 Contrary to the common perception of Mahatma Gandhi not giving full time to his children due to the busyness, Bapu his grandchildren, sons
 putravadhuon samet parivaar ke sabhi logon kii choti choti baton kaa dhyaan rakhte the
 Mahatma Gandhi's great-granddaughter Neelam Parikh mentioned in the book 'jahan Rao, Mahkate Raho', based on Bapu's collection of letters, that despite all the busyness, Gandhiji used to guide his sons and daughters-in-law through his letters
 And gave them their valuable suggestions
 gandhi patr vyavhaar ke jariye niyamit rup se bacchon se sampark main rahete the or vah bacchon se bhi patr kii ummid rakhte the
 Bapu wrote to his son Harilal, 'no one reads your letter, such is your wish, but nothing is secret in the letters
 tumhaare bare main sab log jaananaa chahenge to ashram ke logon ke liye ek aisa patr tumhen jarur likhnaa chahie
 He further wrote, 'no matter how unhappy i am, i keep waiting for your letters
 mujhe maah main ek patr likhane or ek patr paane kaa haq he
 'bapu writes,' You sacrificed my experiment as i happened and you became 'ba'
 ba samaj gai, isliye ba ne jo paaya vah anya stri ne nahin paaya

 ) Subhash Chandra Bose is one of the great heroes of the country who sacrificed his life for the freedom struggle
 unke sangharshon or desh seva ke jazbe ke kaaran hi mahatma gandhi ne unhen deshbhakton kaa deshbhakt kaha tha
 Learn 10 things of Subhash Chandra Bose
 
 
 1
 Subhash Chandra Bose was born on 23 January 1897 in Cuttack, Odisha
 unke pita kaa naam janakinath bose or maa kaa naam prabhavati tha
 Jankinath was a famous lawyer of Cuttack
 2
 After completing primary education in Cuttack, he enrolled in Ravensha Collegiate School
 jiske baad unhone kalakatta uniwarsity se padhai kii
 In 1919, he passed his BA examination from the first class, he was ranked second in the university
 3
 His father wanted Subhash to become ICS
 unhone apane pita kii yah ichha puri kii
 He got the fourth position in the 1920 ICS examination but Subhash was not inclined to work under the British
 22 april 1921 ko unhone is pad se tyaagptr de diya
 4
 subhash chandra bose kii pehali mulaakaat gandhi ji se 20 july 1921 ko hui thi
 On the advice of Gandhiji, he started working for the Indian freedom struggle
 5
 When he became the principal officer of the Calcutta Municipality, he changed the English name of the routes of Calcutta to the Indian name
 6
 Along with India's independence, their involvement in social work also remained
 bengal kii bhayankar baadh main ghire logon ko unhone bhojan, vastra or surakshit sthanon par pahunchane kaa sahaspurn kaam kiya tha
 To keep the work of social service going on regularly, he established a 'yuva Dal'
 7
 They were trying to get Bhagat Singh released from the gallows
 unki rihaai ke liye unhone gandhi ji se baat kii or kaha ki rihaai ke mudde par kiya gaya samjhauta ve angrejon se tod den
 Under this agreement, the release of Indian prisoners from jail was sought
 gandhi ji british sarkaar ko diya gaya vachan todane ke liye raji nahin hue, jiske baad bhagat singh ko faansee de di gai
 After this incident he became very angry with the way Gandhi and Congress functioned
 8
 Subhash was sentenced to a total of 11 times in his public life
 sabase pehle unhen 16 july 1921 ko chah maheene kaa karawas diya gaya tha
 He was scheduled to appear in a Calcutta court in connection with a case in 1941, when he left his home and reached Germany
 germany main unhone hitler se mulaakaat kii
 He formed the Azad Hind Fauj to wage war against the British and also gave the slogan of 'you give me blood, i will give you freedom'
 9
 1934 AD main subhash apana ilaaj karaane ke liye austria gaye the
 At that time, he needed a typist to write his book
 unhen emily shenkal naam kii ek typist mahila mili
 Subhash married this typist in 1942
 10
 On 18 August 1945, he was going to Manchuria by airplane
 is safar ke dauraan taihoku hawaii adde par vimaan durghatnagrast ho gaya, jisamen unki maut ho gai
 His death remains the biggest mystery in the history of India
 unki rahasyamayi maut par samay-samay par kai tarah kii atakalein saamne aati rahati hai
 Two days before the Supreme Court heard the petitions challenging the National Judicial Appointments Commission Act, the Union Government on Monday implemented the controversial law in relation to the appointment of members in the High Judiciary
 rashtriya nyaayik niyukti ayog (engeesi) or samvidhan sanshodhan adhinium (99waan sanshodhan adhinium) ko aaj se prabhavi banane vaali adhisuchana vidhi mantralay main nyaay vibhaag dwaara jari kii gai
 With this, the new entity has got constitutional status
 khaas baat yah he ki jari karne ke 48 ghanton ke baad yah maamla ek baar phir supreme court jayega jahaan par is notificesh ko radd karne kii maang kii ja rahi he
 It is noteworthy that a constitution bench of 5 judges has been made in the Supreme Court to hear the National Judicial Appointments Commission (NJAC) Act
 ye peeth 15 april ko maamle kii sunwaayee shuru karegi
 On April 7, the double bench of the Supreme Court while sending the matter to the Constitution Bench, said that the matter of banning the law should be placed before the Constitution Bench
 vakeelon kii kai sansthaaon ne supreme court main yachikaayen daayar kar chunauti di thi
 These petitions stated that the appeal was repealed by declaring the NJAC Act as arbitrary and unconstitutional
 yachika main kaha gaya ki isse nyaayadhishon kii niyukti main karypalika kaa dakhal badhegaa jisase nyaaypalika kii swatantraaa or nishpakshta prabhavit hogi
 During the hearing, the Central Government had justified this in the court, saying that the Supreme Court can hear the matter right now because the notification has not been issued for it
 yachika main kaha gaya tha ki nyaayik niyukti ayog kanoon or 121waan samvidhan sanshodhan kanoon nirast kiya jaae, kyonki isse supreme court or hoicourt main nyaayadhishon kii niyukti main karypalika kaa hastkshep badhata he, jo na sirf nyaaypalika kii swatantraaa ko baadhit karata he balki samvidhan ke mul dhaanche ko bhi prabhavit karata he jisamen swatantra nyaaypalika kii baat kahi gai he
 The Judicial Appointments Commission will be headed by the Chief Justice of India
 unke alaava supreme court ke do varisht nyaayadhish, kanoon mantri or do vikhyath hastiyaan hongi
 Two eminent personalities will be selected by a three-member committee
 is samiti main pradhanmantri, mukhya nyaayadhish or loksabhaa main netaa vipaksh yaa sabase bade vipakshi dal ke netaa honge
 Section 5 (6) of the law says that if two members of the commission do not agree to appoint someone, then the commission will not recommend the appointment of that person
 yachikakarta kaa kahana he ki iskaa sidhaa matlab he ki mukhya nyaayadhish ke najariye ko nazarandaaj kiya ja saktaa he, jabaki supremecourt kii nau nyaayadhishon kii samvidhan peeth edwocket on record maamle main kah chuki he ki nyaayadhishon kii niyukti main mukhya nyaayadhish kii raay nazarandaaj nahin kii ja sakati, jabaki naye kanoon ke mutabik ayog kaa alp samooh (do sadsy) aisa kar sakate hai
 The new law does not decide what will be the merit of two eminent persons, nor is it decided from which field they will be elected while these two members will have the right to change the opinion of the remaining four members

 ' Diwali (diwali 2018) is the biggest festival of Hindus

, in which the festival of Bhai Dooj (bhai Dooj 2018) is celebrated on the last day
 is tithi se yamraj or dwitiya tithi kaa sambandh hone ke kaaran isko yamadvitiya bhi kaha jaataa he

 is baar bhai dooj kaa parv 09 navambar ko manaaya jayega
 What is the process of worship for Bhai Dooj? - On this day, see Bhai Moon in the morning
 - iske baad yamuna ke jal se snaan karen yaa tajejalse snaan karen
 - Go to your sister's house and get food made from sister's hands there
 - bahanen bhai ko bhojan karaaen or unka tilak karke aarti karen
 - Give the gift to your sister as brother wishes
 koun hainchitragupta maharajaur kya he inaki mahima?- chitragupta ji kaa janm brahma ji ke chitt se hua tha
 - Their task is to keep a book according to the deeds of beings
 - mukhya rup se inaki poojabhidooj ke din hoti he
 - Worshiping them gives the boon of writing, speech and learning
 is din chitragupta ji kii upasna kaise karen ?- praatah kaal purv disha main chowk banaaen
 - Establish Chitragupta Bhagwan's Deity on it
 - unke samaksh ghi kaa deepak jalaaen, pushp or mishthann arpit karen
 - Offer them a pen as well
 - iske baad ek safed kaagaj parahaldilgakar us par "shri ganeshy namah" likhen
 - Then write "om Chitragupta Namah" 11 times
 -bhagavaanchitrgupta se vidya,buddhi or lekhan kaa vardaan maangen
 - Preserve the pen offered and used throughout the year
